				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Also hat Gott die Welt geliebt, BWV 68 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Also hat Gott die Welt geliebt
</td></tr>

<td>5 movements:
<ol><li> Choral: Also hat Gott die Welt geliebt
</li><li> Aria (soprano): Mein gläubiges Herze
</li><li> Recitativo (bass): Ich bin mit Petro nicht vermessen
</li><li> Aria (bass): Du bist geboren mir zugute
</li><li> Chorus: Wer an ihn gläubet, der wird nicht gerichtet
</li></ol>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>Perhaps published earlier? The aria "Mein gläubig[es] Herze" was published in 1853 (see <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://anno.onb.ac.at/cgi-content/anno-buch?apm=0&amp;aid=1000001&amp;bd=0001853&amp;teil=0203&amp;seite=00000391&amp;zoom=1">Hofmeister's <i>Monatsbericht</i> (1853), p.391</a></span> - one assumes this is the same Bach aria). - Schissel
</li></ul>
<ul><li>The movements 1 and 4 are arrangements of the movements 13 and 7 of <a href="/wiki/Was_mir_behagt,_ist_nur_die_muntre_Jagd,_BWV_208_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Was mir behagt, ist nur die muntre Jagd, BWV 208 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)"><b>BWV 208</b></a> (Jagd cantata). 
</li></ul>
